<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Court for the District of Massachusetts as <i><font style="font-style:italic;">In re:&nbsp;&nbsp; Pharmaceutical Industry Average Wholesale Price
Litigation, MDL 1456.</font></i>&#160; During
the second quarter, twenty-two New York counties filed lawsuits in federal
courts in New York that have been or will be transferred to MDL 1456.&#160; These twenty-two New York counties along with
nine other previously disclosed New York counties filed a master consolidated
complaint.&#160; In addition to the previously
disclosed investigations, the Texas Attorney General is investigating Abbott&#146;s
marketing and pricing practices with respect to certain reimbursable
pharmaceutical products, and the Department of Justice is contemplating a civil
proceeding against an unspecified number of other pharmaceutical companies and
Abbott in connection with its investigation, which is more fully discussed in
Abbott&#146;s 2004 Form 10-K.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In its 2004 Form 10-K, Abbott reported that the court
in <i><font style="font-style:italic;">In re: Lupron</font></i>&#174; <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Marketing and Sales Practices Litigation</font></i>, <i><font style="font-style:italic;">MDL 1430</font></i>, had granted preliminary approval
for a proposed nationwide settlement of litigation involving allegations that
TAP Pharmaceutical Products Inc. (TAP) reported false pricing information in
connection with Lupron&#174;.&#160; On May 12, 2005,
the United States District Court for the District of Massachusetts gave its
final approval to that settlement, under which TAP will pay $150 million.&#160; Additionally, the claims of most of the
plaintiffs who sought to be excluded from the nationwide settlement were also
settled, with TAP paying no more than an additional $12.24 million.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In its Form 10-Q for the first quarter of 2005, Abbott
reported that six cases were pending in which Abbott sought to protect the
patents covering fenofibrate, a drug Abbott sells under the trademark
TriCor&#174;.&#160; During the second quarter, all
of these cases, other than <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Reliant</font></i>,
were resolved through mutual releases, except for counterclaims by two parties,
Teva and Impax.&#160; Additionally, Abbott
paid approximately $1.75 million in costs.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the second quarter, ten lawsuits, including
nine purported class actions, were filed against Abbott, Fournier Industrie et
Sante, and Laboratoires Fournier, S.A. (Fournier) in the United States District
Court for the District of Delaware alleging antitrust and unfair competition
claims in connection with the sale of fenofibrate formulations.&#160; The nine purported class actions are:&#160; <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Allied
Services Division Welfare Fund and Hector Valdes, </font></i>filed in June
2005; <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Diana Kim on behalf of herself and
others similarly situated, </font></i>filed in June 2005; <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Louisiana Wholesale Drug Company, Inc.,</font></i>
filed in May 2005; <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Meijer, Inc. and Meijer
Distribution, Inc.,</font></i> filed in June 2005; <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Painters District Council No. 30 Health and Welfare Fund and Richard G.
Wilde, </font></i>filed in June 2005; <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Pennsylvania
Employees Benefit Trust Fund, </font></i>filed in June 2005; <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Elaine M. Pullman, Neil Perlmutter, Helena Perlmutter
and Lula Ramsey, </font></i>filed in June 2005; <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Rochester Drug Co-Operative, Inc.,</font></i> filed in June 2005; and <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Vista Healthplan, Inc. and Ross Love, </font></i>filed
in June 2005.&#160; The individual lawsuit is:
<i><font style="font-style:italic;">Walgreen Co.; Eckerd Corporation; The Kroger
Co.; and Maxi Drug, Inc., </font></i>filed in June 2005.&#160; These cases seek actual damages, treble
damages and other relief.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In its Form 10-Q for the first quarter of 2005, Abbott
reported that it is a defendant in numerous lawsuits involving the drug
oxycodone, a drug manufactured and sold by Purdue Pharma under the trademark
OxyContin&#174;.&#160; Abbott promoted OxyContin to
certain specialty</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">physicians, including surgeons and anesthesiologists, under a
co-promotion agreement with Purdue Pharma.&#160;
Most of the lawsuits allege generally that plaintiffs suffered personal
injuries as a result of taking OxyContin.&#160;
A few lawsuits allege consumer protection violations and unfair trade
practices. One suit by a third party payor alleges antitrust pricing violations
and overpricing of the drug. As of June 30, 2005, a total of 191 lawsuits are
pending in which Abbott is a party.&#160; 27
cases are pending in federal court.&#160; 164
cases are pending in state court.&#160; 180
cases are brought by individual plaintiffs, and 11 cases are brought as
purported class action lawsuits.&#160; Purdue
Pharma is a defendant in each lawsuit and, pursuant to the co-promotion
agreement, Purdue is required to indemnify Abbott in each lawsuit.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In its Form 10-Q for the first quarter of 2005, Abbott
reported that it is a defendant in a number of lawsuits involving the drug
sibutramine (sold under the trademarks Meridia&#174;, Reductil&#174;, Reductyl<sup>TM</sup>,
and Reductal<sup>TM</sup>) that have been brought either as purported class
actions or on behalf of individual plaintiffs.&#160;
The lawsuits generally allege design defects and failure to warn.&#160; Certain lawsuits also allege consumer
protection violations and/or unfair trade practices.&#160; During the second quarter, Abbott resolved
pending state and twelve federal lawsuits for $14.75 million.&#160; In the second quarter, Abbott was notified
that an additional case, <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Leathers, </font></i>was
filed in the United States District Court for the District of Massachusetts.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In its Form 10-Q for the first quarter of 2005, Abbott
reported that it is involved in five cases pending in the United States
District Court for the Northern District of Illinois related to Abbott&#146;s
patents for clarithromycin (a drug Abbott sells under the trademarks Biaxin&#174;,
Biaxin&#174;XL, Klacid&#174;, and Klaricid&#174;).&#160; In
one of those cases, Abbott obtained a preliminary injunction against Teva in
June 2005 preventing Teva&#146;s launch of its extended release clarithromycin
product.&#160; Teva has appealed that decision.&#160; Two other parties, Andrx and Ranbaxy, have
agreed not to launch their extended release clarithromycin products before the
court issues a decision on Abbott&#146;s requests for preliminary injunctions, which
are expected in September 2005.&#160; During
the second quarter, Abbott and Ranbaxy settled their litigation relating to
Ranbaxy&#146;s immediate release formulation.&#160;
Ranbaxy will license certain patents in exchange for royalty payments.
Litigation related to Abbott&#146;s clarithromycin patents is also pending in the
Netherlands, Belgium, Ireland, Turkey and Canada.&#160; Abbott has resolved the previously reported
litigation in the United Kingdom and Spain.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In June 2005, Abbott filed a lawsuit against Takeda Pharmaceutical
Company Limited and Takeda America Holdings, Inc. (&#147;Takeda&#148;) in the United
States District Court for the Northern District of Illinois alleging Takeda
breached its fiduciary duty to Abbott in that Takeda is diverting to itself
profits that rightly belong jointly to Abbott and Takeda as equal joint venture
partners in TAP Pharmaceutical Products Inc. (owned 50 percent by Abbott and 50
percent by Takeda).&#160; Abbott seeks
injunctive relief, and compensatory and punitive damages.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On April 27, 2005, the United States District Court for the Northern
District of</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Illinois
denied Abbott&#146;s motion to dismiss the plaintiffs&#146; complaint in <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Myla Nauman, Jane Roller and Michael Loughery v.
Abbott Laboratories and Hospira, Inc., </font></i>a purported class action
lawsuit filed on November 8, 2004.&#160; The
plaintiffs are former Abbott employees who allege their transfer to Hospira,
Inc., as part of the spin-off of Hospira, adversely affected their employee
benefits in violation of the Employee Retirement Income Security Act.&#160; Plaintiffs generally seek reinstatement as
Abbott employees, or reinstatement as participants in Abbott&#146;s employee benefit
plans, or an award for the employee benefits they have allegedly lost.&#160; Abbott has filed a response denying all
substantive allegations.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Five cases are pending related to Abbott&#146;s patents for
sevoflurane (an anesthesia product Abbott sells under the trademarks Ultane&#174;
and Sevorane&#174;).&#160; In June 2005, Baxter
Healthcare Corporation and Baxter Healthcare Ltd. sued Abbott and Central Glass
Company, Ltd. in the United Kingdom, High Court of Justice, seeking a
declaration that Baxter&#146;s proposed generic sevoflurane product does not
infringe Abbott&#146;s patents.&#160; In May 2005,
Abbott and Central Glass sued Baxter Company, Ltd. in the Tokyo District Court
in Japan, alleging Baxter&#146;s proposed generic sevoflurane product infringes
their formulation patent.&#160; Two cases
brought by Abbott and Central Glass against Baxter Healthcare Corporation are
pending in the United States District Court for the Northern District of
Illinois alleging Baxter&#146;s proposed generic sevoflurane product infringes their
formulation patents.&#160; One additional case
is pending in the Sao Paulo State Court in Brazil, where </font>Abbott and Central Glass allege a
generic sevoflurane product sold by Cristalia Productos Quimicos Farmaceuticos,
Ltda. infringes their formulation patent.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">While it is not feasible to predict the outcome of
such pending claims, proceedings and investigations with certainty, management
is of the opinion that their ultimate dispositions should not have a material
adverse effect on Abbott&#146;s financial position, cash flows, or results of
operations.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">21</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

  <td width="15%" valign="bottom" style="border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:15.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">36,848,000</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="3%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:3.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-24.0pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>These
shares represent:</p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-24.0pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-24.0pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
shares surrendered to Abbott to satisfy tax withholding obligations in
connection with the vesting of restricted stock &#150; 10,363 in April, 0 in May,
and 11,787 in June;</p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-24.0pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
shares deemed surrendered to Abbott to pay the exercise price and to satisfy
tax withholding obligations in connection with the exercise of employee stock
options &#150; 416,733 in April, 331,844 in May, and 381,634 in June; and</p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-24.0pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-24.0pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iii)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
shares purchased on the open market for the benefit of participants in the
Abbott Canada Stock Retirement Plan &#150; 10,000 in April, 10,000 in May, and
10,000 in June.</p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-24.0pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-24.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>On
October 14, 2004, Abbott announced that Abbott&#146;s board of directors approved
the purchase of up to 50 million of its common shares.</p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 44.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 44.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">NOTE:&#160; For the purpose of calculating this ratio,
(i) earnings from continuing operations have been calculated by adjusting
earnings from continuing operations for taxes on earnings from continuing
operations; interest expense; capitalized interest cost, net of amortization;
minority interest; and the portion of rentals representative of the interest
factor, (ii) Abbott considers one-third of rental expense to be the amount
representing return on capital, and (iii) fixed charges comprise total interest
expense, including capitalized interest and such portion of rentals.</font></p>

<div>

<h6 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit
31.1</font></b></h6>

<h6 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h6>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Certification
of Chief Executive Officer</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Required by Rule 13a-14(a) (17 CFR 240.13a-14(a))</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">I, Miles D. White, certify that:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">I
have reviewed this quarterly report on Form 10-Q of Abbott Laboratories;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">Based
on my knowledge, this report does not contain any untrue statement of a
material fact or omit to state a material fact necessary to make the statements
made, in light of the circumstances under which such statements were made, not
misleading with respect to the period covered by this report;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">Based
on my knowledge, the financial statements, and other financial information
included in this report, fairly present in all material respects the financial
condition, results of operations and cash flows of Abbott as of, and for, the
periods presented in this report;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">Abbott&#146;s
other certifying officer and I are responsible for establishing and maintaining
disclosure controls and procedures (as defined in Exchange Act Rules 13a-15(e)
and 15d-15(e)) and internal control over financial reporting (as defined in
Exchange Act Rules 13a-15(f) and 15d-15(f)) for Abbott and have:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">a)</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">Designed
such disclosure controls and procedures, or caused such disclosure controls and
procedures to be designed under our supervision, to ensure that material information
relating to Abbott, including its consolidated subsidiaries, is made known to
us by others within those entities, particularly during the period in which
this report is being prepared;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">b)</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">Designed
such internal control over financial reporting, or caused such internal control
over financial reporting to be designed under our supervision, to provide
reasonable assurance regarding the reliability of financial reporting and the
preparation of financial statements for external purposes in accordance with
generally accepted accounting principles;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">c)</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">Evaluated
the effectiveness of Abbott&#146;s disclosure controls and procedures and presented
in this report our conclusions about the effectiveness of the disclosure
controls and procedures, as of the end of the period covered by this report
based on such evaluation; and</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">d)</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">Disclosed
in this report any change in Abbott&#146;s internal control over financial reporting
that occurred during Abbott&#146;s most recent fiscal quarter that has</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\vmaniraj\05-13789-1\task519554\13789-1-ma.htm',USER='vmaniraj',CD='Aug  3 19:40 2005' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">materially
affected, or is reasonably likely to materially affect, Abbott&#146;s internal
control over financial reporting; and</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">Abbott&#146;s
other certifying officer and I have disclosed, based on our most recent
evaluation of internal control over financial reporting, to Abbott&#146;s auditors and
the audit committee of Abbott&#146;s board of directors:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">a)</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">All
significant deficiencies and material weaknesses in the design or operation of
internal control over financial reporting which are reasonably likely to
adversely affect Abbott&#146;s ability to record, process, summarize and report
financial information; and</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">b)</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">Any
fraud, whether or not material, that involves management or other employees who
have a significant role in Abbott&#146;s internal control over financial reporting.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div>

<h6 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 31.2</font></b></h6>

<h6 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></h6>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Certification of Chief Financial Officer</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Required by Rule 13a-14(a) (17 CFR
240.13a-14(a))</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">I, Thomas C. Freyman, certify that:</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">I
have reviewed this quarterly report on Form 10-Q of Abbott Laboratories;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">Based
on my knowledge, this report does not contain any untrue statement of a
material fact or omit to state a material fact necessary to make the statements
made, in light of the circumstances under which such statements were made, not
misleading with respect to the period covered by this report;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">Based
on my knowledge, the financial statements, and other financial information
included in this report, fairly present in all material respects the financial
condition, results of operations and cash flows of Abbott as of, and for, the
periods presented in this report;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">Abbott&#146;s
other certifying officer and I are responsible for establishing and maintaining
disclosure controls and procedures (as defined in Exchange Act Rules 13a-15(e)
and 15d-15(e)) and internal control over financial reporting (as defined in
Exchange Act Rules 13a-15(f) and 15d-15(f)) for Abbott and have:</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">a)</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">Designed
such disclosure controls and procedures, or caused such disclosure controls and
procedures to be designed under our supervision, to ensure that material information
relating to Abbott, including its consolidated subsidiaries, is made known to
us by others within those entities, particularly during the period in which
this report is being prepared;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">b)</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">Designed
such internal control over financial reporting, or caused such internal control
over financial reporting to be designed under our supervision, to provide
reasonable assurance regarding the reliability of financial reporting and the
preparation of financial statements for external purposes in accordance with
generally accepted accounting principles;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">c)</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">Evaluated
the effectiveness of Abbott&#146;s disclosure controls and procedures and presented
in this report our conclusions about the effectiveness of the disclosure
controls and procedures, as of the end of the period covered by this report
based on such evaluation; and</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">d)</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">Disclosed
in this report any change in Abbott&#146;s internal control over financial reporting
that occurred during Abbott&#146;s most recent fiscal quarter that has materially
affected, or is reasonably likely to materially affect, Abbott&#146;s internal
control over financial reporting; and</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">a)</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">All

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">b)</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font face="Times New Roman">Any
